# 5 UV Ceti - Tau Ceti
uv_ceti_system = {
	name = "NAME_UV_Ceti"
	class = sc_binary_m_m						
	asteroid_belt = {
		type = rocky_asteroid_belt
		radius = 60
	}
	max_instances = 1
	flags = { sol_sector }
	
	
	planet = {									
		name = "NAME_UV_Ceti"								
		count = 1								
		class = pc_m_star								
		orbit_distance = 25								
		orbit_angle = 0								
		size = 23								
		has_ring = no								
	}

	planet = {									
		name = "NAME_BL_Ceti"								
		count = 1								
		class = pc_m_star								
		orbit_distance = 15
		orbit_angle = 180	
		size = 22								
		has_ring = no																						
	}
	
	change_orbit = 20
	
	planet = {
		count = { min = 1 max = 4 }
		class = pc_asteroid
		orbit_distance = 0
		orbit_angle = { min = 0 max = 360 }
	}
	
	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 15 max = 20 }
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
		
		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}
	
	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 20 max = 30 }
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
		
		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}

	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 30 max = 40 }
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
		
		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}
	
	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 40 max = 50 }
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
		
		change_orbit = @base_moon_distance

		moon = {
			count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
			orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }
			orbit_distance = 5
		}
	}

	neighbor_system = {
		distance = { min = 10 max = 40 }
		initializer = "tau_ceti_system"
	}
}

	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 55 max = 65 }
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }	
	}
	
	planet = {
		count = { min = 0 max = 1 }
		orbit_distance = { min = 65 max = 75 }
		orbit_angle = { min = 90 max = 270 }	
	}
	
	init_effect = {
		create_amoeba_country = yes
		random_system_planet = {
			limit = { is_star = no }
			event_target:amoeba_country = {
				create_fleet = {
					name = "NAME_Space_Amoeba"
					effect = {
						set_owner = event_target:amoeba_country
						while = {
							count = 8
							create_ship = {
								name = ""
								design = "NAME_Small_Space_Organism_Teal"
							}
						}
						while = {
							count = 2
							create_ship = {
								name = ""
								design = "NAME_Large_Space_Organism_Teal"
							}
						}
						set_location = PREVPREV
						set_fleet_stance = aggressive
						set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
						set_aggro_range = 100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
